<UserId.>100807811825163549938< /UserId.><name>Lora Taber</name>< Date>
1550423515191<//Date>
< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< review>
For what this place is, it's perfect. It's not fine dining by any stretch. The inside of the place is small, holding only four small tables. The pasties are amazing! The crust is unbelievably light and flakey. The filling is steamy and flavorful. I had a Bavarian pasty, which has ground beef, cabbage, and bell pepper. My companion had a vegan pasty, all vegetable filling. Whatever spices they use made both taste great. We each got the optional gravy, which is vegan. It's a British brand called Bisto. We also got a side of coleslaw, which was good (Solomon's Deli in Davis has the best coleslaw I've ever had, and this wasn't quite that good), and canned soda, Pellegrino. The service is extremely fast. You can grab a pasty and go for a quick meal. We decided to eat there, and were the only customers from about 12:30 - 1:00 on a Saturday. I sure hope they do more business on weekdays. Go if you can, because it would be a shame if a place this great went out if business!< /review>

Fun spot. It was a big quiet on labor day weekend, but the pool table was amazing. Only $0.75! Can't beat it. The drinks were good also - the bartender was quick and courteous since it was just our party pretty much.

<user>108104332502818441606< /user><name>Mike Viens<//name><date>1548529833026<//date><Rate>1< /Rate>< review>
The only plus I see, is it is located in Folsom. The bagels are not very good, and they are over-priced. I ordered a dozen bagels, and was disappointed that it was 12 instead of the traditional 13 for a baker's dozen. While paying, the cashier must have been new (which is ok, we all learn when doing a new job) because she got scolded by an angry woman for not charging enough. Evidently having a cranberry bagel means it is "gourmet" and therefore needs a higher price. I was told the new amount was $18.47. I said there is no way I was paying that for a dozen bagels. The angry woman again scolded this young worker who was getting frustrated. I felt bad for her. A third worker came to help her out. The new total was $16 and some change. Still way too much money for twelve bagels. All because I did not want to drive an extra 15 minutes (each way) to go to Noah's on Hazel. I figured the bagels would still be good. I get home and we start to eat them. The first raisin bagel tastes like garlic and onion and is covered in sesame seeds. I am fine with the seeds but not a big fan of garlic and, for me, onions taste terrible. Back to the "gourmet" cranberry bagel...while it had a nice taste, the bagels was much smaller than the other flavors I got.  Even the texture of the all the bagels is off. They are very dense, not light and chewy like nearly every other bagel place. Bottom line, they are expensive and poor quality. Sacramento is not known for having good bagels anyway, so if you are looking for something reasonable, go with Noah's. Posh bagel is just a complete disappointment.< /review>

Friendly Service, Great Bagels, Amazing Sandwiches, Good Coffee & Fantastic Pastries!

The owners and staff are very friendly and efficient. They have a large selection of delicious Breakfast and Lunch Sandwiches. Their Bagel & Lox Sandwich is the best I've had. Their breakfast sandwiches will make you never want to look at fast-food breakfast again. They also make their own fresh Pastries, Danishes & Cupcakes. Their hand decorated Cupcakes are impressive. Can't say enough about this hidden treasure.</review>

This is the worst restaurant experience that we have encountered. I normally don't give any bad reviews, especially during COVID 19 since the restaurants and wineries are facing a challenging time. <Time>1597697471602<//Time>< rating>
5< /rating>
<text>Justin is a premium winery with excellent tasting options and food which will match any high end restaurant.

Located in the middle of the Paso Robles vineyards, it‚Äôs an excellent scenic drive to their establishment. When you arrive, you drive on loose gravel and are greeted by a welcoming staff.

Besides the excellent wine, the staff here are exceptional and very geared towards making your stay that much more enjoyable. You‚Äôre treated like royalty.

The seating area is booked right up against the vineyards which makes for a wonderful viewing. When tasting wine, it gives you a great sensation of tasting what you can see and makes you imagine the process of turning the grapes into the succulent nectar of wine, From farm to wine glass.

Price wise it is expensive, but they offer an excellent deal where for ever $100 you spend on wine bottles to go, the tasting fee ($35-$55) is completely waived. This made for an excellent tasting experience and if you plan on getting bottles to go, makes it a no brainer to do the bottles to go.

This is my personal favorite winery of all time and over the years, each wine has failed to disappoint. Their blends make for an exceptional tasting experience where taste buds are taken on a journey from a light hearted rose to a full bodied blend which takes you to euphoria.

Definitely a must for Paso Robles and is always on my list anytime I find myself in the area.</text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMUM5ny0ZbdDyjKs32-zoaMqDCHtAY5Eu_ucDsl=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMJd1AKBEhGF5L34jUgoL3UW-hjS-SUCTlnwoRo=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO50AgMLeETJxDCj0-eBf04zUjLmCGtm3m2kbi_=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures>< Resp>

<Resp>None</Resp>< Review>
The wine is excellent.
The tasting facility is very beautiful and new, you are enveloped by the allure of wine and vineyard.
Our hostess Krystal was as sweet and down to earth as she could be and made us feel very comfortable.
The wine was absolutely lovely.
We tasted out on the "upper patio" and quickly learned that no tasting was allowed on the lower patio in the sun (it was chilly outside), that was our first indication of "not friendly".
Finished our tasting, my friend went into the tasting room/gift shop to use the restroom. I stayed outside for a few moments and followed there after.
As soon as I entered the tasting room a man approached me, and curtly asked if he could help me.
Honestly, I felt like I was trespasser in the way he addressed me!
(I am 63 years old, well dressed, and unassuming)
Good lawd...and then approached by another man in almost the same fashion. Really took me by surprise...these people need to chill.
That being said, the tasting atmosphere at Justin is very snooty and almost paranoid.
If you can get past that, the wine is fabulous.< /Review>

<Text>Love the view here, and it's always full of people from LA and the Bay. It's nestled in a beautiful valley outside Paso Robles, and the drive there is a thrill for those who enjoy winding curvy roads with blind curves and blind hills. There are moments when you literally creat a hill and you don't know if the road will curve to the right or left or if there'll be a drop of several feet. Beautiful road. The winery itself has great ambience, and is family friendly to a degree. Their outdoor seating is comfortable and tables are far apart from each other to afford some privacy and ensures nobody feels bothered by another group. Truly lovely corner of California here.</Text>< user_id>

<time>1546902601653<//time>< review>
If there was a way to give no stars for my recent experience at Justin Winery I would.  I decided to take my entire office staff on a wine tasting trip for their Christmas Party.  I had never been to Justin Winery, so this winery was the one that I was most excited to visit.  When we arrived, luckily, it was not very busy.  There were maybe 5 tables outside and 5 people inside the winery tasting room.  We sat down and waited to be greeted.  When our wine representative came over to the table, Gregory, he was less than friendly.  He did not smile, nor did he try and talk with us to see why we were there, the reason for the visit, etc.  He also did not explain the wines that we would be tasting.  We got our first pour of wine after about 10 to 15 minutes of waiting.  During this time, one of my staff members told Gregory that one of his family members wanted to join the wine club.  Of course, he immediately started working on that on the phone inside.  After we waited and waited for our second pour of wine, one of my employees finally had to go into the actual building and ask for a second pour from another wine representative.  When, Gregory finally finished his phone call and came out with the second pour of wine, he made a comment about my staff member that went into the building to ask for our second pour.  After rolling his eyes, he stated, "Well if she would just quit hounding me" I would come out here and pour wine.  This was the first time anyone had went inside the building.  Gregory was unprofessional, extremely rude, and an outright negative individual.  I have no idea how he would even be able to obtain a job such as this.  Because of my experience with Gregory, I may never go back to Justin.  It is too bad because the wine is very nice!< /review>

< userid>
106206511677592870990< /userid>
< Text>
The BFF is such a fan of Justin Vineyard and after our tasting experience, I get it now.  Party of 13 please....

We stopped in on a hot Saturday afternoon and Larry was our tasting guide.   He was friendly, professional and we learned plenty about the wines we sampled as well as the Justin Vineyard and history.  We had rookies and seasoned Wine veterans and Justin worked well with both.
Our tasting included:
2016 Viognier - Light, refreshingly perfect for the hot day.
2016 Reserve Cabernet Sauvignon - Best Cabernet I've tasted this year.
2016 Reserve Tempranillo - Dark, deep, tasty.
2016 Reserve Malbec - Love Malbecs and this might be my new fav.  I purchased two bottles as souvenirs
2015 Isoceles Reserve - Award winner, lovely and I'll be stashing a bottle at home.

The lobby and showroom is spacious and organized well.  They have plenty of Justin items that covers souvenirs, apparel, to wine accessories of course.  You can also pick up some snacks, cheese, crackers to add to your tasting experience.

In the patio there's some great patio seating with great view of this lovely property with the vines and the mountains in the distance.  There are definitely plenty of social media moments here.  If in the area, Justin is a definite visit to enjoy some great wine and make even greater memories.  Cheers!< /Text>

0x80ed29f7f823a82d:0xb550b7414f39c66d< /gmapID>
< Rate>
4</Rate>
<text>JUSTIN Vineyards and Winery is a beautiful place to stop for wine tasting, lunch, and a winery tour. The tasting room and restaurant stands out like a contemporary ranch house amongst the surrounding vineyards. Row upon row of vines stretch across the land and hills like fine stitch work. If you decide to stay for lunch, here are a few suggestions from the menu:

A great way to try the wines while enjoying a meal is with a flight. The White Wine Flight includes 2014 JUSTIN Sauvignon Blanc, 2014 JUSTIN Ros√©, and 2013 Landmark Overlook Chardonnay. The Sauvignon Blanc has a pear nose. Green apple and peach flavors are experienced on the palate with a light, clean finish. Rating: 3.5/5. The Ros√© has a blackberry and cherry aroma. Strawberry and grapefruit flavors are experienced on the palate with a nice, clean finish. Rating: 4.5/5. The Chardonnay has a white grape and pear aroma. White grape, pear, floral, and mineral flavors experienced on the palate. Rating: 2.5/5

Windrose Farm Lamb Tartare is topped with garden greens, preserved lemon aioli, and crostini. This was a fantastic take on tartare. The lamb was sweet and minced perfectly. The use of shaved egg yolk added a richness to the dish without the mess of a runny egg yolk. The fresh greens from the garden paired nicely. Rating: 4.5/5

JUSTIN Fries are tossed with truffle salt, parmesan, and JUSTIN fine herb blend. The fries were light and crispy. The truffle flavor was just right so the parmesan and herbs could shine as well. Rating: 4.5/5

Bucatini Pasta tossed with Alle-Pia sausage, wild mushrooms, bitter greens, smoked butter, and parmesan. This was an excellence lunch dish, light yet satisfying. The sauce had a rich creamy texture. The flavors of the succulent mushrooms and lean, meaty sausage balanced perfectly with the sauce and pasta. Rating: 4.5/5

JUSTIN Brownies topped with caramel, cocoa nibs, and served with lemon balm ice cream. The brownie was served warm with rich, decadent chocolate flavor. Caramel sauce made the dish more luxurious. The lemon balm ice cream was refreshing with unexpected herbal notes. It was different and made a nice contrast to the brownie. Rating: 3.8/5

After lunch, a walking tour is a great way to burn some calories. JUSTIN Vineyards and Winery offers tours of their facility. Be sure to call ahead for a reservation as the tours are limited to 10 people per tour. Our tour guide, Larry, took us around the winery, showing us the machinery used to mill and press the grapes during harvest and the large stainless steel tanks used for the fermentation process. He then walked us through the caves where the different wines are aged in French Oak barrels. You will also be tasting wine along the way - Ros√©, Merlot, Petit Syrah, and Reserve. You'll also notice that scattered around the vineyard are poles with metal boxes on top. They sort of look like large bird houses. They are homes for the owls who rid the vineyards of rodents and snakes. They let nature take on the job of pest control so chemical pesticides are not used.

After the tour, head back to the tasting room to sample and purchase your favorite wines. Take a walk around the on-site vegetable garden where they grow the produce that is ultimately going to end up on your plate in the restaurant - kale, different varieties of lettuce, edible flowers, Swiss chard, and more. Lady bugs and praying mantis are also natural pest controllers and are on patrol here as well.< /text>< user>
